			SELECT 
				hour,
			    MAX(`energy`) AS peak_energy,
			    ROUND(AVG(`energy`),4) AS avg_engery
			    
			FROM
				 `householddb` 
		
			SELECT *
			FROM
				 `householddb`
			WHERE energy < (SELECT
			    				ROUND(AVG(`energy`),4) 
							FROM
			    				`householddb`
			               )
			ORDER BY energy ASC
